As a SaaS platform, Partnerize gives us direct contact with our partners allowing for clearer lines of communication. The commissioning tools have assisted us to test and experiment with some really exciting things. The team at Partnerize are the true highlight though - such a friendly and supportive team who have gotten back to all issues and enquires quickly and to a high standard. Love working with them! <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about Partnerize?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Previously the Data analytics section of Partnerize was not entirely helpful to our goals but this has been recently updated and is now fantastic. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-4641952 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">Recommendations to others considering Partnerize:</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Make sure to have a resource available to manage the Partnerize platform. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-4641952 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is Partnerize solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">One of the key benefits of Partnerize for us is having direct communications with all of our partners allowing for transparency. Real-time data has also been greatly beneficial to us. The platform is easy to use and saves us time in reporting. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex justify-between"><a class="link href="https://www.g2.com/products/partnerize/reviews/partnerize-review-4352507"><div class="m-0 l2" itemprop="name">"Partnerize was able to quickly grow with our businesses complex needs for international growth."</div></a></div><div data-poison-text=""><div itemprop="reviewBody"><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you like best about Partnerize?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Partnerize was able to source the relationships they needed in order to pay partners around the world along with establish international offices so we could continue to grow. Parnterize also had established relationships with account management vendors that could support our program. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about Partnerize?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Our partnership has always been very responsive and we've rarely had any problems with Partnerize. Anything that was brought to their attention was handled quickly and professionally. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-4352507 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">Recommendations to others considering Partnerize:</div><div><p class="formatted-text">The Partnerize team is building their tools on the most modern, efficient, and fast technology available. The other platforms have a long way to go to migrate their old systems into the modern era. If you are planning on running a program with many points of data, you need fast systems that can accurately manage and report on that data too.  The older platforms could not support the reporting needs of our team. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-4352507 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is Partnerize solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Our partnerships needed to expand beyond the limited set of countries we serviced with other platforms. Partnerize was by our side from the very beginning to bring their platform to over 150 countries where we do business. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex justify-between"><a class="link d-f ai-c x-show-more js-log-click x-toggle-class-initialized x-login-modal-toggle-initialized" ue="toggle-class Another big win is how granular we can get with our commissioning, to be able to set a different commission rate for a set of SKU's really helps us to drive higher conversion on stock we need to sell. This allows me to hit my overall KPIs when combined into blended stats with other marketing channels. I typically reward new visitor focused partners more aggressively than those at the lower funnel levels - in relation to the overall LTV that is brought in. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about Partnerize?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">I haven't found any downsides yet! Will let you know when I do. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-4353895 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is Partnerize solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">The ability to get high level insights along with granular reporting with ease through the reporting  interface. I wasn't able to find anyone else to match Partnerize on this level. I need different types of reporting and data points based on the departments I work with, Partnerize allows me to satisfy the needs of all levels of the business. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex justify-between"><a class="link d-f ai-c x-show-more js-log-click x-toggle-class-initialized" ue="toggle-class login-modal-toggle" Partnerize is rock solid on that account. The C-Level team is very engaged. However, that engagement does not seem to be part of the platform at a cultural level. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about Partnerize?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">On, what seems to be a quarterly basis, we will have a technical issue with some change on the platform that requires technical support. Every time that's happened the support has been either nonexistent or very slow. Additionally documentation when it comes to the API is terrible. Basic functionality that we would expect to find in an affiliate network (I realize Partnerize is more) is just not available in the UI. Reporting is overly complicated to pull. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-4357281 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">Recommendations to others considering Partnerize:</div><div><p class="formatted-text">None at this time. It's to general of a question. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-4357281 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is Partnerize solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Partnerize's ability to white label its solution has been very helpful. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex justify-between"><a class="link d-f ai-c x-show-more js-log-click x-toggle-class-initialized" ue="toggle-class The platform enables us to understand the types of customers we are driving and we can therefore optimise our content strategy accordingly based on our most effective promotions. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about Partnerize?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">The partner side user interface could do with a refresh. Sometimes the data in the reporting tab defaults back to the original settings when applying filters which is a bit of a bug. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-4212630 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">Recommendations to others considering Partnerize:</div><div><p class="formatted-text">I would say you can't go far wrong if you're an advertiser considering Partnerize to manage your affiliate or partnership program. Just ensure you have enough resource internally to fully manage your own program as this is a SaaS platform, not an affiliate network. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-4212630 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is Partnerize solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Partnerize is a fully automated partnership system.  For affiliates like us with hundreds of different advertisers, the ability to postback information in real-time to our own reporting system is invaluable. The automated payment system also means we don't need to chase advertisers individually for payment, saving us several hours of admin time every month. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex justify-between"><a class="link d-f ai-c x-show-more js-log-click x-toggle-class-initialized" ue="toggle-class login-modal-toggle" Mobile tracking has helped us capture a lot more sales to the platform, which was important to us. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about Partnerize?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">You definitely need to go to that first training session. The key plus items are highly flexible, lots of options, and  allows us to commission in ways we never could before. The mobile tracking has helped us capture a lot more sales to the platform, which was important to us.. On the negative side, you definitely need to go to that first training session. Without the guide though it can seem daunting. But it's not hard once use it a couple of times. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-4245647 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is Partnerize solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Using their system, managing international programs has been much more streamlined.
